Celebrated in Dubai.\\n \\nOn the occasion of the Abu Dhabi F1 Grand Prix, Berluti revealed its Spring-Summer 2023 collection in Dubai among friends of the House, such as \u0040alpinef1team Driver \u0040estebanocon, \u0040abdulla, \u0040twistedcurlz and \u0040danclemt to name a few.\\n \\nThere is a more fluid and relaxed feel to Berluti\u2019s iconic ready-to-wear, leather goods and footwear such as the new Lorenzo car shoe for Spring-Summer 2023, yet the Maison\u2019s legacy of bootmaking still shines through. Throughout its succession of fabrics and accessories, the patterns, colours and textures serve to showcase a wardrobe that marries strong lines and formally cut tailoring with functional dimensions. THE #BERLUTI SPRING-SUMMER 2023 COLLECTION -\\n\\nCreated in Paris. Celebrated in Dubai.\\n\\nOn the occasion of the Abu Dhabi F1 Grand Prix, Berluti revealed its Spring-Summer 2023 collection in Dubai among friends of the House, such as \u0040alpinef1team Driver \u0040estebanocon, \u0040abdulla, \u0040twistedcurlz and \u0040danclemt to name a few.\\n\\nThere is a more fluid and relaxed feel to Berluti\u2019s iconic ready-to-wear, leather goods and footwear such as the new Lorenzo car shoe for Spring-Summer 2023, yet the Maison\u2019s legacy of bootmaking still shines through. Its artistry with fine leathers, patinas and colours was the guiding principle behind this collection of contemporary silhouettes imbued with timeless elegance. Throughout its succession of fabrics and accessories, the patterns, colours and textures serve to showcase a wardrobe that marries strong lines and formally cut tailoring with functional dimensions. Berluti continues to demonstrate its love of noble materials and pushes attention to detail to its very apogee. \\n\\nThe collection includes also a capsule dedicated to golf.\\n\\nThe Spring-Summer 2023 collection will be soon available in-store and on the e-shop.\\n\\nPhotographies by \u0040virgile.guinard
